Eduar do Ferreira Pres. of Sicr edi Biomasţ 8«Âsªƕsƕ¤¾s«s 33 years developing local communities: On January 29, 1989, S icredi Biomas began its activities in the city of Araputanga-MT, with 23 founding partners and, in the beginning, it was called the Rural Credit Cooperative of the Northwest of Mato Grosso – Credinoroeste. At the beginning, the idea of ​​the cooperative was to encourage and support small rural producers in the region. In 1997, the Cooperative joined the Sicredi Credit System and was renamed Sicredi Noroeste MT. A few years later, in 2009, the name change of the Cooperative was approved to “Free Admission Credit Cooperative for Members of the Northwest of MT”. During an assembly held in 2015, members approved the start of the expansion of activities for the state of Acre. Five years later, there was also the ordeal to take the Cooperative's products and services to the state of Amazonas, once again causing the name to change, which is now called Sicredi Biomas MT AC A M. In 2021 we surpassed the 50 thousand associates and we opened our first agency in the state of Amazonas, located in Guajará. Today, with 33 years of experience, in 2021 we managed more than 2 billion reais and c We have more than 52 thousand members. We are present in three Brazilian states. We are present in three Brazilian states, Acre, Amazonas and Mato Grosso, with branches in 25 municipalities. By 2025, we aim to reach the goal of more than 100,000 members and open 25 more Sicr edi Biomas branches in the states in which we operate. And this will only be possible with the active participation of all our associates. 33 years developing local communities: On January 29, 1989, S icredi Biomas began its activities in the city of Araputanga-MT, with 23 founding partners and, in the beginning, was called Rural Credit Cooperative of Noroeste de Mato Grosso – Credinoroeste. At the beginning, the idea of ​​the cooperative was to encourage and support small rural producers in the region. In 1997, the Cooperative joined the Sicredi Credit System and was renamed Sicredi Noroeste MT. A few years later, in 2009, the name change of the Cooperative was approved to “Free Admission Credit Cooperative for Members of the Northwest of MT”. During an assembly held in 2015, members approved the beginning of the expansion of activities to the state of Acre. Five years later, there was also the ordeal to take the Cooperative's products and services to the state of Amazonas, once again causing the name to change, which now passes Call Sicredi Biomas MT AC A M. In 2021 we surpassed the mark of 50 thousand members and opened our first agency in the state of Amazonas, located in Guajará. Today, with 33 years of operation, in 2021 we managed more than 2 billion reais and have more than 52 thousand members. We are present in three Brazilian states. We are present in three Brazilian states, Acre, Amazonas and Mato Grosso, with branches in 25 municipalities. By the year 2025, we aim to reach the goal of more than 100,000 members and open another 25 Sicr edi Biomas branches in the states in which we operate. And this will only be possible with the active participation of all our associates. As usual, in the first semester of each year the process of reporting of Sicredi Biomas to its members and deciding the direction of the Cooperative. In 2021, due to the Covid-19 pandemic, the Assembly was held in a hybrid format, where members were able to vote at branches and through the website. And, in this way, we had an excellent result in participation in this edition. O number of members who voted on the proposals, 7,634, was 73.2% higher compared to the 2020 blear assembly period. In relation to the 2020 blear membership base. In relation to the previous year's membership base, reaching 19% participation . In 2020, 4,406 members voted, which represented 13% of the member base. The agendas presented and put to a vote were: accountability for the year 2020, extension of the term of office of Core Coordinators – term of office of president, allocation, distribution of results, attendance card for counselors, auditing standards, compliance policy and strategic planning of the Cooperative. Within the agenda there were suggestions given by members during the Cooperative Chat that was held the previous month. Regarding the extension of the mandate of Core Coordinators, the Board of Directors (CONSAD) proposed that the mandate be extended until 2022. Regarding the destination of the results obtained In 2020, members decided that 100% of the available amount – more than 14 million reais – would be allocated to the Current Account. Regarding the distribution of results, it was decided that 20% would be allocated to a demand deposit, 10% to a time deposit (Sicredi Invest), 20% Poupança Sicredi, 5% to a relationship basket, 10% to a collection slip, 15 % in commercial credit (consigned loans, financing, personal credit, etc.), 10% for consortium, 10% for credit card and M aquininha Sicredi. This year there was the election of Center Coordinators in the city of Cruzeiro do Sul-AC, where for Center 1 the following were elected: Donário Lima Cordeiro as effective coordinator and Ariane Hinca C. Perim and Janaína V. G. Terças as substitutes. In Core 2, the following were elected: Núcia Sales de Melo as effective coordinator and José Luiz G. da Costa and Marcelli M. de Oliveira as substitutes. ƕ ±ªsÂ ƕ PP 8 2 & ƕŠŞŠşƕƕ As usual, in the first semester Each year, Sicredi Biomas' accountability process is carried out to its members and the direction of the Cooperative is decided. In 2021, due to the Covid-19 pandemic, the Assembly was held in a hybrid format, where members were able to vote at branches and through the website. And, in this way, we had an excellent result in participation in this edition. The number of members who voted on the proposals, 7,634, was 73.2% higher compared to the 2020 white assembly period. in relation to the blear membership base in 2020. In relation to the previous year's membership base, reaching 19% participation. In 2020, 4,406 members voted, which represented 13% of the member base. The agendas presented and put to a vote were: accountability for the year 2020, extension of the term of office of Core Coordinators – core coordinators, term of office of president, allocation, distribution of results, attendance ballot for counselors, auditing standards, auditing policy compliance and strategic planning of the Cooperative. Within the agenda there were suggestions given by members during the Cooperative Chat that was held the previous month. Regarding the extension of the mandate of Core Coordinators, the Board of Directors (CONSAD) proposed that the mandate be extended until 2022. Regarding the allocation of the results obtained in 2020, the members decided that 100% of the available amount – more than 14 million reais – would be allocated to the Current Account. Regarding the distribution of results, it was decided that 20% would be allocated to a demand deposit, 10% to a time deposit (Sicredi Invest), 20% Poupança Sicredi, 5% to a relationship basket, 10% to a collection slip, 15 % in commercial credit (payroll deductible, financing, personal credit, etc.), 10% for consortium, 10% for credit card and M aquina Sicredi. This year there was the election of Center Coordinators in the city of Cruzeiro do Sul-AC, where to Core 1 were elected: Donário Lima Cordeiro as effective coordinator and Ariane Hinca C. Perim and Janaína V. G. Terças as substitutes. In Core 2, the following were elected: Núcia Sales de Melo as effective coordinator and José Luiz G. da Costa and Marcelli M. de Oliveira as substitutes. IL? Is«±¾sªsƕ±ƕI¾±¾sªsƕ Z«|±ƕ sâƕsƕcs ŠŞŠŞŠŞşŧ ŠŞŠşŠŞŠŞŠŞşŧ ŠŞŠşChildren and adolescents participating ŠŞŠŞŠ Şşŧ ŠŞŠşEducator and participant ŠŞŠŞŠŞşŧ ŠŞŠşMunicipalities impactedParticipating schools şŞŸţŞť şšŸšŤŞ şşŸŢŧŧ ťŠŧ ŦťŦ şŸ šŠťŢţ ţŠ Ţš Ţ Ť ţThe União Faz a Vida Program is Sicredi's main education program and aims to build and experience attitudes and values ​​of cooperation and citizenship. The program's main investment is the continued training of educators with a focus on developing a specific project methodology. Is«±¾sªsƕ±ƕI¾±¾sªsƕ Z«|±ƕ sâƕsƕcs ŠŞŠŞŠŞşŧ ŠŞŠşŠŞŠŞŠŞşŧ ŠŞŠşChildren and adolescents participating ŠŞŠŞŠ Şşŧ ŠŞŠşEducator is par participants ŠŞŠŞŠŞşŧ ŠŞŠşImpacted municipalitiesParticipating schools şŞŸţŞť şšŸšŤŞ şşŸŢŧŧ ťŠŧ ŦťŦ şŸšŠťŢţ ţŠ Ţš Ţ Ť ţThe União Faz a Vida Program is Sicredi's main education program and aims to build and experience attitudes and values ​​of cooperation and citizenship. Sicredi Biomas currently runs the program in five cities: Araputanga, Comodoro, Pontes e Lacerda and São José dos Quatro Marcos, in Mato Grosso and Cruzeiro do Sul, in Acre. The program's main investment is the continued training of educators with a focus on developing a specific project methodology. Other investments are also made in communication, recognition actions for educators, education commemorative dates and in the formation of the Pedagogical Advisory team that accompanies the Program in the region. & ƕ ƕ Z9 ?ƕP? & 2şŦ L¤s ±«sª«È±ƕƕ ±±»¾sÈÖÂª± (It's from the heart, it's cooperation) In addition to developing social responsibility actions, the campaign aims to put into practice the values ​​and principles of cooperativism, helping society and minimizing the impacts of economic and social inequality. The fundraising actions were simultaneous in all Cooperativ a agencies and the community was invited to donate non-perishable food, with Sicredi Biomas donating the same quantity, generating more strength for the action, so to serve more people, a mutual action of solidarity between and cooperative and the community. For the president of Sicredi Biomas, Eduar do Ferreira, the campaign was a success due to the participation of the population, which is fundamental in this act of solidarity. “This Campaign shows the strength of cooperativism. Sicredi is made by people for people and has the objective of building an increasingly prosperous, fair and participatory society. In addition, we continue to operate the movements “People who Cooperate Care” and “I Cooperate with the Economy Local" , which helped us take care of people and communities, rĚîǶƑŞîŠēū the strength of cooperativism as an engine capable of contributing to the continuity of economic activity in the country. Traditionally, Sicredi collects food that is donated to families in need. In 2021, Sicredi Biomas carried out the campaign It's from the heart, it's cooperation and collected around 50 tons of food that were distributed in all municipalities where we operate. The action also included collection of toys and books With the aim of serving non-profit private entities, since 2020 Sicredi Biomas has made part of the ǶŠîŠČĚĿƑ part available. In 2021, Sicredi Biomas served more than 70 entities in our area of ​​operation in MT, AC and cities in our area of ​​operation in MT, AC and real for the acquisition of various items such as wheelchairs, biosafety materials, basic food baskets and personal hygiene, as well as other items. Various entities such as APAEs, Rotarys, Lions, Children's Homes and Homes for the Elderly were assisted with the Social Fund. Everything that comes from Sicredi starts from a common starting point: doing it together. We believe that the strength of the collective makes the world a better place. Therefore, cooperation is fundamental when supporting causes. If the cause was born in the same way as us, from people who came together to make a difference, what does it have to do with us? At the beginning of 2021, the state of Acre suffered from floods that flooded and destroyed several cities, leaving thousands of people homeless. Sicredi Biomas, with the support of the local community, can also help the families most affected by the tragedy. Sena Madureira Paulo Ricar do, which was one of the cities most impacted by the floods, received resources from the Social Fund so that families could be helped during this period. & ƕ ƕ Z9 ?ƕP? & 2şŦ L¤s ±«sª«È±ƕƕ ±±»¾sÈÖÂª± (It's from the heart, it's cooperation) In addition to develop social responsibility actions, the campaign aims to put into practice the values ​​and principles of cooperativism, helping society and minimizing the impacts of economic and social inequality. LÂÍ¤Ès±ƕŲƕƕŢųŦƕ~ ¤¹ÂƕWe have been operating for over 115 years promoting transformation in the lives of our associates and the local community. We currently have more than 5.5 million members and are present in all regions of Brazil with more than 2.1 thousand branches, distributed in more than 100 cooperatives We have more than 30 thousand employees and are among the Best Companies for You to Work For the ninth consecutive time. This data is from Você S/A magazine. We understand that the best choices are those that bring results for everyone. We offer more than 300 products and services in a simple and close way for you, your company and your agribusiness. But what makes us different is that when you join, you acquire a small share of your cooperative, becoming the owner of Sicredi, having a voice over business decisions and participating in the results. That's why Sicredi is yours, mine and ours. In 2020 we were ranked in Exame Magazine's Melhores & Maiores as the second institution with the highest release of rural credit. In this report you will have information on how we generate all results while maintaining our values ​​and purpose. ƕsƕ¤3⁄4s«s Reaching 2022 with so many conquests achieved, despite all the difficulties faced, is a source of great satisfaction for all of us. However, we can say that our greatest achievement is seeing the satisfaction and appreciation of our associates. We have been operating in communities for 33 years, providing products and services that meet the needs of the local reality in a sustainable way and promoting social development. That is our purpose. For us, being increasingly closer to our members is of utmost importance, which is why we adopted and maintained throughout 2021 projects that bring the C operative closer together. of the community, such as the President's Table, the moment for nucleus coordinators at the Board of Directors meetings, the Cooperative Chat and the Assembly, which demonstrate that our desire is to listen and gather the needs of our members, to that together we can achieve even more impactful results. We hope that in 2022 more people will have the opportunity to get to know Sicredi Biomas and be part of this business model that values ​​the associate and the community. communities. You are very important for the future of Sicredi Biomas. We count on you! Strong hug! Eduar do Ferreira Pres. of Sicr edi Biomasţ 8«Âsªƕsƕ¤¾s«s 33 years developing local communities: On January 29, 1989, S icredi Biomas began its activities in the city of Araputanga-MT, with 23 founding partners and, in the beginning, it was called the Rural Credit Cooperative of the Northwest of Mato Grosso – Credinoroeste. At the beginning of everything, the idea of ​​the cooperative was encourage and support small rural producers in the region. In 1997, the Cooperative joined the Sicredi Credit System and was renamed Sicredi Noroeste MT. A few years later, in 2009, the name change of the Cooperative was approved to “Free Admission Credit Cooperative for Members of the Northwest of MT”. During an assembly held in 2015, members approved the beginning of the expansion of activities to the state of Acre. Five years later, There was also an ordeal to take the Cooperative's products and services to the state of Amazonas, once again causing the name to change, which is now called Sicredi Biomas MT AC A M. In 2021 we surpassed the mark of 50 thousand members and we opened our first agency in the state of Amazonas, located in Guajará. Today, with 33 years of operation, in 2021 we managed more than 2 billion reais and have more than 52 thousand members. We are present in three Brazilian states. We are present in three Brazilian states, Acre, Amazonas and Mato Grosso, with branches in 25 municipalities. By 2025, we aim to reach the goal of more than 100 thousand members and open another 25 Sicr edi Biomas branches in the states in which we operate. And this will only be possible with the active participation of all our associates. ĂƉƌĞƐĞŶƚĂĚŽŶĂEKd ϯϮ͘ ƐͿDŽĞĚĂĨƵŶĐŝŽŶĂůŠŦƕL¤sÈ²¾±ƕ «Ís¤ŠŞŠşţ 8«Âsªƕsƕ¤¾s«s 33 years developing local communities: On January 29, 1989, S icredi Biomas began its activities in the city of Araputanga-MT, with 23 founding partners and, in the beginning, it was called the Rural Credit Cooperative of the Northwest of Mato Grosso – Credinoroeste. At the beginning, the idea of ​​the cooperative was to encourage and support small rural producers in the region. In 1997, the Cooperative joined the Sicredi Credit System and became known as Sicredi Noroeste MT. A few years later, in 2009, the name change of the Cooperative was approved to “Free Admission Credit Cooperative for Members of the Northwest of MT”. During an assembly held in 2015, members approved the beginning of the expansion of activities to the state of Acre. Five years later, there was also the ordeal to take the Cooperative's products and services to the state of Amazonas, once again causing a change in the name, which is now called Sicredi Biomas MT AC A M. In 2021 we surpassed the mark of 50 thousand members and opened our first agency in the state of Amazonas, located in Guajará. Today, with 33 years of operation, in 2021 we managed more than 2 billion reais and have more than 52 thousand members. We are present in three Brazilian states.We are present in three Brazilian states, Acre, Amazonas and Mato Grosso, with branches in 25 municipalities.9±ÂÂsƕ ±±»¾sÈÖs P ¾ƕ ±ªsÂ By the year 2025, we aim to reach the goal of more than 100 thousand members and open 25 more Sicr edi Biomas branches in the states in which we operate . And this will only be possible with the active participation of all our members. LÂÍ¤Ès±ŲƕƕŢųŦƕ~¤¹Âƕ ªƕsÈÖ±ÂŲƕƕŠƕ~¤¹Âƕ ªƕ ¾È±Ųƕƕşų Ťƕ~¤¹ A ŞŠş P ¾ƕ ±ªsÂ ÂÈs½ÍÂƕP ¾ƕ ±ªsÂƕªƕŠŞŠşƕ The Future Marathon 2021 was an event inspired by Ideathon and H ackathon type methodologies, which brought together people interested in the topics proposed, with the aim of solving common problems. They were Two axes were worked on: The expansion of Co-operativism in the State of Acre and the selective collection and treatment of waste in the city of Rio Branco – A C. The participants were organized into teams looking for the best solution for these two themes. The two best evaluated teams, according to the selection criteria, were awarded R$50,000.00 each for the execution of the projects during 2022. ϭϮ͘ϳϵϵ ϭϳ͘ϭϲϬ ŽƚĂÉ ĚĞ ĨƵŶĚŽÉ ĚĞ ƌĞŶĚĂ ĮǆĂ Ğ ŵƵůƟŵĞƌĐĂĚŽ Two axes were worked on: The expansion of Co operativism in the State of Acre and selective collection and waste treatment in the city of Rio Branco – A C. Participants organized themselves into teams looking for the best solution for these two themes. The two best evaluated teams, according to the selection criteria, were awarded R$50,000.00 each for the execution of the projects during 2022 8s¾sÈ±«sƕ ÍÈÍ¾±Ŧ &«È¾±Í |± ±¾ªs|±ƕ»s¾sƕ ¾«ÈÂ ƕ9² ±Â ½ÍƕUªƕUs¤«È±I¾±¡È±ƕLsâ Â The Raízes project aims to carry out a technical assistance and rural extension program for rural and/or agro-industrial enterprises and development of projects and proposals to obtain financial support through financing to be carried out by Sicredi Biomas, in all agencies in its area of ​​operation. The objective of supporting collective or individual actions to add value, optimize family work, use technologies and access markets for family farming products. The project completed in 2021 13 families and will last 4 years, with expansion expected. The project arose from the need to train and expand the skills of employees in the business area (Business Managers) on a better commercial approach and sales techniques. The training was carried out between July and December 2021 and brought together around 40 employees. develop projects and proposals to obtain financial support through financing to be carried out by Sicredi Biomas, in all agencies of its occupation area. The objective of supporting collective or individual actions to add value, optimize work family, use of technologies and access to markets for family farming products. The project served 13 families in 2021 and will last 4 years, with plans to expand. The project arose from the need to train and expand the skills of employees in the business area (Business Managers) on a better commercial approach and management techniques. sales. The training was carried out between July and December 2021 and brought together around 40 employees. It is a project focused on providing more clarity about internal growth opportunities at Biomas, providing opportunities for all employees who meet the requirements « sƕc¾ÈÍs¤ In 2021 we began the process of centralizing W hatsApp Enterprise services, via virtual agency. Before that, services through the application were carried out by business managers at physical branches. As a result, in addition to facilitating the flow of face-to-face services, this transformation brought reducing member waiting times through mobile service. On average, the virtual agency can quickly serve around 2000 members per month. &«È¾±Í|± ±±»¾s«±ƕ«sƕ s¤ss Cooperating on the sidewalk was born from the need to bring members closer to our agencies. Our employees stood at strategic points in the city presenting S icredi Biomas and offering our products and services in a lighter and more relaxed way. The project was implemented by the Buriti de Pontes e L acerda-MT agency between the months of May and September and provided an increase of approximately 45% in new members. previously defined, can compete for these vacancies. The project also includes feedback to participants in the evaluation process, which takes place through a panel formed by Biomas leaders. The project brought with it a greater number of internal opportunities, greater clarity about what is needed to take on GA positions Agency Manager, GN Business Manager, GAF Administrative Manager Our employees stood at strategic points in the city presenting S icredi Biomas and offering our products and services in a lighter and more relaxed way. The project was implemented by the Buriti de Pontes e L acerda-MT agency between the months of May and September and provided an increase of approximately 45% in new members. previously defined, can compete for these positions. The project brought with it a greater number of internal opportunities, greater clarity about what is needed to take on the roles of GA Agency Manager, GN Business Manager, GAF Financial Administrative Manager, among others. ŧ şŞƕƕƕL¤sÈ²¾±ƕ «Ís¤ ŠŞŠş P ¾ƕ ªsÂ ƕ PP 8 2 & ƕŠŞŠşƕƕ As As usual, in the first half of each year, Sicredi Biomas' accountability process is carried out to its members and the direction of the Cooperative is decided. In 2021, due to the Covid-19 pandemic, the Assembly was held in a hybrid format, where members were able to vote at branches and through the website. And, in this way, we had an excellent result in participation in this edition. The number of members who voted on the proposals, 7,634, was 73.2% higher compared to blear assembly period of 2020. In relation to the 2020 blear membership base. In relation to the previous year's membership base, reaching 19% participation. In 2020, 4,406 members voted, which represented 13% of the member base. The agendas presented and put to a vote were: accountability for the year 2020, extension of the term of office of Core Coordinators – core coordinators, term of office of president, allocation, distribution of results, attendance ballot for counselors, standards auditing, compliance policy and strategic planning of the Cooperative. Within the agenda there were suggestions given by members during the Cooperative Chat that was held the previous month. Regarding the extension of the mandate of Core Coordinators, the Board of Directors (CONSAD) proposed that the mandate be extended until 2022. Regarding the allocation of the results obtained in 2020, the associates decided that 100% of the available amount – more than 14 million reais – were allocated to the Current Account. Regarding the distribution of results, it was decided that 20% would be allocated to a demand deposit, 10% to a time deposit (Sicredi Invest), 20% Poupança Sicredi, 5% to a relationship basket, 10% to a collection slip, 15 % in commercial credit (payroll deductible, financing, personal credit, etc.), 10% for consortium, 10% for credit card and M aquina Sicredi. This year there was the election of Center Coordinators in the city of Cruzeiro do Sul-AC, where the following were elected to Nucleus 1: Donário Lima Cordeiro as effective coordinator and Ariane Hinca C. Perim and Janaína V. G. Terças as substitutes. In 2021, due to the Covid-19 pandemic, the Assembly was held in a hybrid format, where members were able to vote at branches and through the website. And, in this way, we had an excellent result in participation in this edition. The number of members who voted on the proposals, 7,634, was 73.2% higher compared to the blear assembly period of 2020. In relation to the blear membership base in 2020. In relation to the previous year's membership base, reaching 19% of participation. In 2020, 4,406 members voted, which represented 13% of the member base. The agendas presented and put to a vote were: accountability for the year 2020, extension of the term of office of Core Coordinators – core coordinators, term of office of president, allocation, distribution of results, attendance ballot for counselors, audit standards, compliance policy and strategic planning of the Cooperative. Within the agenda there were suggestions given by members during the Chat Cooperative that was held the previous month. Regarding the extension of the mandate of Core Coordinators, the Board of Directors (CONSAD) proposed that the mandate be extended until 2022. Regarding the destination of the results obtained in 2020, the members decided that 100% of the available amount – more than 14 million reais – would be allocated to the Current Account. Regarding the distribution of results, it was decided that 20% would be allocated to a demand deposit, 10% to term deposit (Sicredi Invest), 20% Poupança Sicredi, 5% for relationship basket, 10% for billing slip, 15% in commercial credit (consigned loan, financing, personal credit, etc.), 10% for consortium, 10% for credit card and M aquina Sicredi. This year there was the election of Nucleus Coordinators in the city of Cruzeiro do Sul-AC, where for Nucleus 1 the following were elected: Donário Lima Cordeiro as effective coordinator and Ariane Hinca C. Perim and Janaína V. G. Terças as substitutes. In Core 2, the following were elected: Núcia Sales de Melo as effective coordinator and José Luiz G. da Costa and Marcelli M. de Oliveira as substitutes.IL? L8 ƕ L P ¾“Here we also developed a Crescer program whose main objective is to disseminate knowledge about cooperativism and Sicredi, creating commitment and forming a support base for business continuity.” Crescer program offers training that expands understanding of the functioning of a cooperative society and the role of members in the governance of a cooperative, helping to form new leaders. In 2021, despite the challenges imposed by the Covid-19 pandemic, Sicredi Biomas trained more than 6 thousand people with the Program. Opportunities were generated through hybrid training: online and in-person. The program directly follows the lives of members after training and provides information that shows the transparency of the business model, which further proves the credibility and transparency of Sicredi Biomas. L8 ƕ L P ¾“Here we also developed a Crescer program whose main objective is to disseminate knowledge about cooperativism and Sicredi, creating commitment and forming a support base for business continuity.”Through the Crescer program, we offer training that expands understanding of the functioning of a cooperative society and the role of members in the governance of a cooperative, helping to form new leaders. In 2021, despite the challenges imposed by the Covid-19 pandemic, Sicredi Biomas trained more than 6 thousand people with the Program. Opportunities were generated through hybrid training: online and face-to-face. The program directly monitors the lives of members after training and provides information that shows the transparency of the business model, which further proves the credibility and transparency of Sicredi Biomas. Is«±¾sªsƕ±ƕI¾±¾sªsƕ Z«|±ƕ sâƕsƕcs ŠŞŠŞŠŞşŧ ŠŞŠşŠŞŠŞŠŞşŧ ŠŞŠşChildren and adolescents participating ŠŞŠŞŠ Şşŧ ŠŞŠşEducator and participant ŠŞŠŞŠŞşŧ ŠŞŠşMunicipalities impactedParticipating schools şŞŸţŞť şšŸšŤŞ şşŸŢŧŧ ťŠŧ ŦťŦ şŸ šŠťŢţ ţŠ Ţš Ţ Ť ţThe União Faz a Vida Program is Sicredi’s main education program and aims to build and experience attitudes and values ​​of cooperation and citizenship. Sicredi Biomas currently runs the program in five cities: Araputanga, Comodoro, Pontes e Lacerda and São José dos Quatro Marcos, in Mato Grosso and Cruzeiro do Sul, in Acre. The program's main investment is the continued training of educators with a focus on developing a specific project methodology. Other investments are also made in communication, recognition actions of educators, educational commemorative dates and the formation of the Pedagogical Advisory team that accompanies the Program in   3$57,&,3$d®(61$662%5$6 62%5$6 28 3(5'$6 '2 6(0(675( P ¾ ƕ ±ªsÂ IL?L 8 ƕ ƕZ9& ?oƕ ƕc& ƕ For Sicredi, the objective of the program is to develop cooperative citizens, valuing Thus, in 2021, the Program developed more than 200 projects. ŠŞŠşParticipating children and adolescents ŠŞŠŞŠŞşŧ ŠŞŠşParticipating educator ŠŞŠŞŠŞşŧ ŠŞŠşImpacted municipalitiesParticipating schools şŞŸţŞť şšŸšŤŞ ş şŸŢŧŧ ťŠŧ ŦťŦ şŸšŠťŢţ ţŠ Ţš Ţ Ť ţThe A União Faz a Vida Program is Sicredi's main education program and aims to build and experience attitudes and values ​​of cooperation and citizenship. Sicredi Biomas currently runs the program in five cities: Araputanga, Comodoro, Pontes e Lacerda and São José dos Quatro Marcos, in Mato Grosso and Cruzeiro do Sul, in Acre. The program's main investment is the continued training of educators with a focus on developing a specific project methodology. Other investments are also made in communication, recognition actions for educators, education commemorative dates and in the formation of the Pedagogical Advisory team that accompanies the Program in the region. & ƕ ƕ Z9 ?ƕP? & 2şŦ L¤s ±«sª«È±ƕƕ ±±»¾sÈÖÂª± (It's from the heart, it's cooperation) In addition to develop social responsibility actions, the campaign aims to put into practice the values ​​and principles of cooperativism, helping society and minimizing the impacts of economic and social inequality. The fundraising actions were simultaneous in all Cooperativ a agencies and the community was invited to donate non-perishable food, with Sicredi Biomas donating the same quantity, generating more strength for the action, so to serve more people, a mutual action of solidarity between the cooperative and the community. For the president of Sicredi Biomas, Eduar do Ferreira, the campaign was a success due to the participation of the population, which is fundamental in this act of solidarity. “This Campaign shows the strength of cooperativism. Sicredi is made by people for people and has the objective of building an increasingly prosperous, fair and participatory society. In addition, we continue to operate the movements “Gente que Coopera Cuida” and “Eu Coopera com a Economia Local”, which helped us take care of people and communities, reinforcing the strength of cooperativism as an engine capable of contributing to the continuity of economic activity in the country. Traditionally, Sicredi collects food that is donated to families in need. In 2021, Sicredi Biomas carried out the campaign It's from the heart, it's cooperation and collected around 50 tons of food that were distributed in all municipalities where we operate. The action also included the collection of toys and books. With the aim of serving non-profit private entities, since 2020, Sicredi Biomas has made part of the result available. In 2021, Sicredi Biomas served more than 70 entities in our area of ​​operation in MT, AC and cities in our area of ​​operation in MT, AC and real for the acquisition of various items such as wheelchairs, biosafety materials, baskets basic and personal hygiene items, as well as other items. Several entities such as APAEs, Rotarys, Lions, Children's Homes and Homes for the Elderly were assisted with the Social Fund. Everything that comes from Sicredi starts from a common starting point: doing it together. We believe that the strength of the collective makes the world a better place. Therefore, cooperation is fundamental when supporting causes. If the cause was born in the same way as us, from the people who came together to make a difference, that it has to do with us. At the beginning of 2021, the state of Acre suffered from floods that flooded and destroyed several cities, leaving thousands of people homeless. Sicredi Biomas, with the support of the local community, can also help the families most affected by the tragedy. Sena Madureira Paulo Ricar do, which was one of the cities most impacted by the floods, received resources from the Social Fund so that families could be helped during this period. cooperation) In addition to developing actions of social responsibility, the campaign aims to put into practice the values ​​and principles of cooperativism, helping society and minimizing the impacts of economic and social inequality. The fundraising actions were simultaneous in all Cooperativ a agencies and the community was invited to donate non-perishable food, with Sicredi Biomas donating the same quantity, generating more strength for the action, in order to serve more people, a mutual action of solidarity between the cooperative and the community. For the president of Sicredi Biomas, Eduar do Ferreira, the campaign was a success due to the participation of the population, which is fundamental in this act of solidarity. “This Campaign shows the strength of cooperativism. Sicredi is made by people for people and has the objective of building an increasingly prosperous, fair and participatory society. In addition, we continue to operate the movements “People who Cooperate Care” and “I Cooperate with the Economy Local”, which helped us take care of people and communities, rĚîǶƑŞîŠēū the strength of cooperativism as an engine capable of contributing to the continuity of economic activity in the country. Traditionally, Sicredi collects food that is donated to families in need. In 2021, Sicredi Biomas carried out the campaign It's from the heart, it's cooperation and collected around 50 tons of food that were distributed in all municipalities where we operate. The action also included the collection of toys and books. With the aim of serving non-profit private entities, since 2020, Sicredi Biomas has made part of the result available. In 2021 the Sicredi Biomas served more than 70 entities in our area of ​​operation in MT, AC and cities in our area of ​​operation in MT, AC and reals for the acquisition of various items such as wheelchairs, biosafety materials, basic and personal hygiene baskets, in addition to other items. Several entities such as APAEs, Rotarys, Lions, Children's Homes and Homes for the Elderly were assisted with the Social Fund. Everything that comes from Sicredi starts from a common starting point: doing it together. We believe that the The strength of the collective makes the world a better place. Therefore, cooperation is fundamental when supporting causes. If the cause was born in the same way as us, from people who came together to make a difference, what does it have to do with us? At the beginning of 2021, the state of Acre suffered from floods that flooded and destroyed several cities, leaving thousands of people homeless. Sicredi Biomas, with the support of the local community, can also help the most affected families by the tragedy. Sena Madureira Paulo Ricar do, which was one of the cities most impacted by the floods, received resources from the Social Fund so that families could be helped during this period.
